# TEIL Y — ARIA'S VOLLSTÄNDIGE DATEN-PIPELINE

> Von rohem Signal zu handlungsfähiger Intelligenz — jeder Schritt dokumentiert.

---

## Y.1 Daten-Ingestion Layer

### Y.1.1 Alle Datenquellen und ihre Charakteristika

```typescript
interface DataSource {
  name: string;
  type: 'api_poll' | 'webhook' | 'manual' | 'computed';
  frequency: string;
  reliability: number;        // 0-1, historische Zuverlässigkeit
  latency: string;            // Wie aktuell sind die Daten
  volume: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high';
  priority: number;           // 1-10, Wichtigkeit für ARIA
}

const DATA_SOURCES: DataSource[] = [
  {
    name: 'Amazon SP-API Orders',
    type: 'api_poll',
    frequency: 'alle 30 Minuten',
    reliability: 0.99,
    latency: '~30 Minuten',
    volume: 'high',
    priority: 10
  },
  {
    name: 'Amazon SP-API Inventory',
    type: 'api_poll',
    frequency: 'stündlich',
    reliability: 0.98,
    latency: '~1 Stunde',
    volume: 'medium',
    priority: 9
  },
  {
    name: 'eBay Orders Webhook',
    type: 'webhook',
    frequency: 'echtzeit',
    reliability: 0.97,
    latency: '<1 Minute',
    volume: 'medium',
    priority: 9
  },
  {
    name: 'Otto Partner API Orders',
    type: 'api_poll',
    frequency: 'alle 15 Minuten',
    reliability: 0.96,
    latency: '~15 Minuten',
    volume: 'medium',
    priority: 8
  },
  {
    name: 'GLS ShipIT Tracking',
    type: 'api_poll',
    frequency: 'alle 2 Stunden',
    reliability: 0.94,
    latency: '~2 Stunden',
    volume: 'medium',
    priority: 7
  },
  {
    name: 'Shopify Orders',
    type: 'webhook',
    frequency: 'echtzeit',
    reliability: 0.99,
    latency: '<30 Sekunden',
    volume: 'low',
    priority: 8
  },
  {
    name: 'Mitarbeiter-Interaktionen',
    type: 'computed',
    frequency: 'echtzeit',
    reliability: 1.0,
    latency: 'echtzeit',
    volume: 'low',
    priority: 6
  }
];
```

### Y.1.2 Signal-Normalisierung — Aus verschiedenen Quellen ein einheitliches Bild

Jede Datenquelle liefert Daten in anderem Format. ARIA normalisiert alles in ein einheitliches Schema:

```typescript
// Universelles Order-Schema (plattformunabhängig)
interface NormalizedOrder {
  id: string;                     // Intern generiert
  externalId: string;             // Plattform-spezifische ID
  platform: 'amazon' | 'ebay' | 'otto' | 'kaufland' | 'shopify';
  tenantId: string;
  
  // Zeitstempel (immer UTC)
  orderedAt: Date;
  paidAt: Date | null;
  shippedAt: Date | null;
  deliveredAt: Date | null;
  
  // Betragsangaben (immer in EUR)
  gross: number;
  net: number;
  tax: number;
  platformFee: number;            // Berechnet aus Platform-Prozentsatz
  estimatedProfit: number;        // net - platformFee - estimatedProductCost
  
  // Kunde
  customer: {
    name: string;
    email: string | null;         // Oft maskiert von Plattformen
    address: NormalizedAddress;
  };
  
  // Artikel
  items: NormalizedOrderItem[];
  
  // Status (plattformunabhängig normiert)
  status: 'pending' | 'paid' | 'processing' | 'shipped' | 'delivered' | 'returned' | 'cancelled';
  
  // Originaldata für Debugging
  rawData: Record<string, unknown>;
}
```

### Y.1.3 Echtzeit-Pipeline Architektur

```
DATA FLOW DIAGRAM:

[Externe APIs/Webhooks]
        ↓
[API Gateway / Webhook-Handler]
   - Validierung (Schema, Auth)
   - Rate-Limit-Check
   - Deduplizierung
        ↓
[BullMQ Ingestion Queue]
   - Priority: Critical > High > Medium > Low
   - Retry mit exponential backoff
   - Dead Letter Queue für Failures
        ↓
[Normalisierungs-Worker]
   - Plattform-spezifisches Mapping
   - Datenqualitäts-Check
   - Fehlende Felder auffüllen (geschätzt)
        ↓
[Supabase (PostgreSQL)]
   - Primäre Datenhaltung
   - RLS (Row Level Security) pro Tenant
        ↓
[ARIA Signal-Processor]
   - Anomalie-Erkennung
   - Trend-Berechnung
   - Alert-Generierung
        ↓
[Notification-Router]
   - An welchen Mitarbeiter?
   - Welcher Kanal? (In-App, Push, Email)
   - Batching (Anti-Spam)
        ↓
[Mitarbeiter sieht Alert]
```

---

## Y.2 Feature Engineering — Was ARIA berechnet

### Y.2.1 Alle berechneten Features

ARIA berechnet nicht nur was passiert ist — es berechnet Merkmale die es mithilfe von Machine Learning verwenden kann, um Muster zu erkennen.

```typescript
// Features die täglich für jeden Tenant neu berechnet werden

interface TenantFeatureVector {
  // Verkaufs-Features
  salesVelocity7d: number;           // Einheiten/Tag (7-Tage)
  salesVelocity30d: number;          // Einheiten/Tag (30-Tage)
  salesVelocityTrend: number;        // % Änderung 7d vs. 30d
  
  // Bestandsfeatures
  averageStockoutRisk: number;       // 0-1, gewichteter Schnitt
  inventoryTurnover: number;         // Wie oft dreht sich Lager/Jahr
  deadStockPercentage: number;       // % Artikel ohne Verkauf >90 Tage
  
  // Kanal-Mix
  amazonShare: number;               // % Umsatz Amazon
  ebayShare: number;
  ottoShare: number;
  shopifyShare: number;
  channelConcentration: number;      // Herfindahl-Index (Klumpenrisiko)
  
  // Marge-Features
  averageGrossMargin: number;
  marginTrend: number;               // % Änderung letzter 90 Tage
  topMarginProducts: string[];       // Top-5 SKUs nach Marge
  lowMarginProducts: string[];       // Bottom-5 SKUs nach Marge
  
  // Kunden-Features
  returnRate: number;                // % Retouren
  returnRateTrend: number;
  repeatCustomerRate: number;        // % Wiederkäufer (Shopify)
  averageOrderValue: number;
  
  // Lieferanten-Features
  supplierConcentration: number;     // Wie abhängig von einzelnem Lieferant
  averageLeadTime: number;           // Tage bis Lieferung
  leadTimeVariability: number;       // Standardabweichung Lieferzeit
  
  // Operations-Features
  fulfillmentAccuracy: number;       // % korrekte Lieferungen
  onTimeDeliveryRate: number;
  orderProcessingTime: number;       // Stunden von Bestellung bis Versand
  
  // Wettbewerbs-Features (wenn verfügbar)
  pricePositionIndex: number;        // 0-1 (0=günstigster, 1=teuerster)
  buyBoxWinRate: number;             // Amazon Buy Box %
}
```

### Y.2.2 Saisonalitäts-Modell

```typescript
// ARIA lernt saisonale Muster pro Tenant und Kategorie

interface SeasonalityModel {
  tenantId: string;
  sku: string;
  
  // Wöchentliche Saisonalität (7 Faktoren, Montag-Sonntag)
  weekdayFactors: [number, number, number, number, number, number, number];
  
  // Monatliche Saisonalität (12 Faktoren)
  monthFactors: [number, number, number, number, number, number, 
                 number, number, number, number, number, number];
  
  // Event-basierte Saisonalität
  eventFactors: {
    event: 'christmas' | 'easter' | 'blackFriday' | 'valentinesDay' | string;
    leadDays: number;           // Wie viele Tage vorher steigt Nachfrage
    peakFactor: number;         // Multiplikator auf Baseline
    tailDays: number;           // Wie lange nach Event noch erhöht
  }[];
  
  // Modell-Qualität
  trainingDataPoints: number;   // Wie viele Datenpunkte zum Training
  accuracy: number;             // MAPE (Mean Absolute Percentage Error)
  lastTrainingDate: Date;
  
  // Prediction
  predictedDemand(date: Date): number;
}

// Beispiel: Treppenschutzgitter
const treppenschutzSaisonalitaet = {
  weekdayFactors: [1.0, 0.95, 0.92, 0.94, 0.98, 1.18, 1.24],  // Sa/So höher (Eltern kaufen am Wochenende)
  monthFactors: [0.78, 0.82, 1.12, 1.28, 1.31, 1.18, 0.95, 0.89, 1.05, 1.15, 1.42, 1.38],  // Frühling + Q4 hoch
  eventFactors: [
    { event: 'christmas', leadDays: 45, peakFactor: 1.85, tailDays: 5 },
    { event: 'easter', leadDays: 14, peakFactor: 1.35, tailDays: 3 },
    { event: 'blackFriday', leadDays: 5, peakFactor: 1.60, tailDays: 7 }
  ]
};
```

---

## Y.3 ARIA's Prediction-Engine — Vollständig

### Y.3.1 Demand-Forecasting Model

```typescript
// ARIA's primäres Demand-Forecast-Modell
// Basiert auf: Historische Daten + Saisonalität + Trend + Events

async function forecastDemand(
  tenantId: string,
  sku: string,
  horizonDays: number
): Promise<DemandForecast> {
  
  // 1. Historische Basis (365 Tage wenn verfügbar)
  const history = await getSalesHistory(tenantId, sku, 365);
  
  if (history.length < 30) {
    // Zu wenig Daten — Cluster-Benchmarks nutzen
    return forecastFromClusterBenchmarks(tenantId, sku, horizonDays);
  }
  
  // 2. Trend-Berechnung (linearer Trend)
  const trend = calculateLinearTrend(history);
  
  // 3. Saisonalitäts-Modell laden/trainieren
  const seasonality = await getSeasonalityModel(tenantId, sku);
  
  // 4. Event-Kalender für Forecast-Periode laden
  const events = await getUpcomingEvents(horizonDays);
  
  // 5. Forecast generieren
  const forecast: DailyForecast[] = [];
  
  for (let day = 1; day <= horizonDays; day++) {
    const date = addDays(new Date(), day);
    
    const baselineDemand = calculateBaseline(history, date);
    const trendAdjustment = trend.slope * day;
    const seasonalFactor = seasonality.predictedDemand(date) / seasonality.predictedDemand(new Date());
    const eventAdjustment = calculateEventAdjustment(events, date);
    
    const pointEstimate = baselineDemand * (1 + trendAdjustment) * seasonalFactor * eventAdjustment;
    
    forecast.push({
      date,
      demand: Math.max(0, pointEstimate),
      confidenceLow: pointEstimate * 0.75,    // 25% Unsicherheitspuffer
      confidenceHigh: pointEstimate * 1.35,    // 35% Überschätzungspuffer
      confidence: calculateForecastConfidence(history.length, seasonality.accuracy)
    });
  }
  
  // 6. Reorder-Point berechnen
  const reorderPoint = calculateReorderPoint(forecast, await getLeadTime(tenantId, sku));
  
  return {
    tenantId,
    sku,
    generatedAt: new Date(),
    horizonDays,
    forecast,
    reorderPoint,
    recommendedOrderQuantity: calculateEOQ(tenantId, sku, forecast),
    summary: `${horizonDays}-Tage-Forecast: ${forecast.reduce((s,f) => s + f.demand, 0).toFixed(0)} Einheiten gesamt. Nachbestellung empfohlen wenn Bestand unter ${reorderPoint} Einheiten.`
  };
}
```

### Y.3.2 Anomalie-Detection — Vollständige Implementierung

```typescript
// ARIA's Multi-Layer Anomalie-Erkennung

async function detectAnomalies(tenantId: string): Promise<Anomaly[]> {
  const anomalies: Anomaly[] = [];
  
  // LAYER 1: Statistische Anomalien (Z-Score)
  const metrics = await getCurrentMetrics(tenantId);
  const baselines = await getBaselines(tenantId);
  
  for (const [metric, value] of Object.entries(metrics)) {
    const baseline = baselines[metric];
    if (!baseline) continue;
    
    const zScore = (value - baseline.mean) / baseline.stddev;
    
    if (Math.abs(zScore) > 2.5) {
      anomalies.push({
        type: 'STATISTICAL',
        metric,
        value,
        expected: baseline.mean,
        deviation: zScore,
        severity: Math.abs(zScore) > 4 ? 'critical' : Math.abs(zScore) > 3 ? 'high' : 'medium',
        direction: value > baseline.mean ? 'above' : 'below'
      });
    }
  }
  
  // LAYER 2: Muster-Anomalien (Was normalerweise zusammen passiert, passiert nicht)
  const returnRateAnomaly = await detectReturnRatePattern(tenantId);
  if (returnRateAnomaly) anomalies.push(returnRateAnomaly);
  
  const shipmentDelayAnomaly = await detectShipmentDelayPattern(tenantId);
  if (shipmentDelayAnomaly) anomalies.push(shipmentDelayAnomaly);
  
  // LAYER 3: Business-Rule-Anomalien
  const stockoutImminent = await detectImminentStockouts(tenantId);
  anomalies.push(...stockoutImminent);
  
  const competitorPriceAnomalies = await detectCompetitorPriceChanges(tenantId);
  anomalies.push(...competitorPriceAnomalies);
  
  // LAYER 4: Cross-Signal-Anomalien
  // Wenn mehrere Signale zusammen auftreten → verstärkte Warnung
  const correlatedAnomalies = findCorrelatedAnomalies(anomalies);
  
  return deduplicateAndPrioritize([...anomalies, ...correlatedAnomalies]);
}
```

# TEIL Z — ARIA'S VOLLSTÄNDIGE SQL-IMPLEMENTIERUNG

> Produktionsreife Datenbank-Schemas. Jede Tabelle vollständig mit Kommentaren, Indizes, RLS-Policies.

---

## Z.1 Vollständige Migration — Alle ARIA-Tabellen

```sql
-- =============================================================================
-- ARIA COMPLETE BRAIN MIGRATION
-- Filename: 20260601_000000_aria_complete_brain.sql
-- Description: Vollständiges ARIA Gehirn-Schema für Comentra
-- Author: ARIA Architecture Team
-- Version: 1.0.0
-- =============================================================================

-- ############################################################################
-- SEKTION 1: GEDÄCHTNIS-TABELLEN
-- ############################################################################

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_episodes: Episodisches Gedächtnis
-- Speichert was passiert ist — der "Erfahrungsschatz" von ARIA
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_episodes (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Zeitlicher Kontext
  occurred_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  day_of_week INTEGER,                    -- 0=Montag, 6=Sonntag
  hour_of_day INTEGER,                    -- 0-23
  
  -- Episode-Klassifikation
  episode_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,      -- 'order', 'return', 'supplier_issue', 'customer_complaint', etc.
  category VARCHAR(100),                  -- Unterkategorie
  subcategory VARCHAR(100),
  
  -- Beteiligte Entitäten
  involved_employees UUID[],              -- Welche Mitarbeiter waren beteiligt
  involved_suppliers UUID[],              -- Welche Lieferanten
  involved_customers VARCHAR[],           -- Welche Kunden (extern)
  involved_skus VARCHAR[],               -- Welche Produkte
  involved_channels VARCHAR[],            -- Welche Marktplätze
  
  -- Episode-Inhalt
  title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,            -- Kurztitel
  description TEXT,                       -- Detailbeschreibung
  outcome VARCHAR(50),                    -- 'positive', 'negative', 'neutral', 'unresolved'
  outcome_detail TEXT,                    -- Was war das konkrete Ergebnis
  
  -- Lernen
  lessons_learned TEXT[],                 -- Was hat ARIA gelernt
  pattern_tags VARCHAR[],                 -- Tags für Mustererkennung
  similarity_embedding VECTOR(1536),      -- Semantic Search Vektor (pgvector)
  
  -- Gewichtung
  importance_score NUMERIC(4,3) DEFAULT 0.5,  -- 0.0-1.0
  recall_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,         -- Wie oft wurde diese Episode abgerufen
  last_recalled_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  
  -- Verlinkung
  related_episode_ids UUID[],             -- Verwandte Episoden
  triggered_by_episode_id UUID REFERENCES aria_episodes(id),
  
  -- Volltextsuche
  search_vector TSVECTOR,
  
  -- Metadaten
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Indizes für Performance
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_tenant ON aria_episodes(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_type ON aria_episodes(episode_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_occurred ON aria_episodes(occurred_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_importance ON aria_episodes(importance_score DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_search ON aria_episodes USING GIN(search_vector);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_skus ON aria_episodes USING GIN(involved_skus);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_episodes_employees ON aria_episodes USING GIN(involved_employees);

-- Volltextsuche automatisch updaten
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_episode_search_vector()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
  NEW.search_vector := 
    setweight(to_tsvector('german', COALESCE(NEW.title, '')), 'A') ||
    setweight(to_tsvector('german', COALESCE(NEW.description, '')), 'B') ||
    setweight(to_tsvector('german', COALESCE(array_to_string(NEW.lessons_learned, ' '), '')), 'C');
  NEW.updated_at := NOW();
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER trigger_episode_search_vector
  BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON aria_episodes
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_episode_search_vector();

-- RLS: Jeder Tenant sieht nur seine eigenen Episoden
ALTER TABLE aria_episodes ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY aria_episodes_tenant_isolation ON aria_episodes
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_knowledge: Semantisches Gedächtnis
-- Was Dinge bedeuten — das "Lexikon" von ARIA
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_knowledge (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Wissens-Klassifikation
  knowledge_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    
  -- 'product', 'customer', 'supplier', 'market', 'process', 'company', 'marketplace', 'competitor'
  
  entity_id VARCHAR(255),                 -- ID der referenzierten Entität (SKU, SupplierID, etc.)
  entity_name VARCHAR(500),              -- Name der Entität
  
  -- Wissens-Inhalt
  fact VARCHAR(1000) NOT NULL,            -- Die Tatsache als Satz
  value_numeric NUMERIC,                  -- Falls quantifizierbar
  value_text TEXT,                        -- Falls qualitativ
  unit VARCHAR(50),                       -- Einheit (%, €, Tage, etc.)
  
  -- Herkunft
  source VARCHAR(100),                    -- Woher kommt dieses Wissen
  source_episode_id UUID REFERENCES aria_episodes(id),
  
  -- Verlässlichkeit
  confidence NUMERIC(4,3) DEFAULT 0.5,   -- 0.0-1.0
  evidence_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,       -- Wie viele Beobachtungen
  last_confirmed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  contradicted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,            -- Falls widerlegt
  contradicted_by_id UUID REFERENCES aria_knowledge(id),
  
  -- Zeitabhängigkeit
  valid_from TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  valid_until TIMESTAMPTZ,               -- NULL = dauerhaft gültig
  decay_days INTEGER DEFAULT 90,          -- Tage bis re-validation nötig
  
  -- Suche
  search_vector TSVECTOR,
  semantic_embedding VECTOR(1536),
  
  -- Tags
  tags VARCHAR[],
  
  -- Metadaten
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_tenant ON aria_knowledge(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_type ON aria_knowledge(knowledge_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_entity ON aria_knowledge(entity_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_confidence ON aria_knowledge(confidence DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_search ON aria_knowledge USING GIN(search_vector);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_tags ON aria_knowledge USING GIN(tags);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_knowledge_expiry ON aria_knowledge(valid_until) WHERE valid_until IS NOT NULL;

ALTER TABLE aria_knowledge ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_knowledge_tenant_isolation ON aria_knowledge
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_employee_fingerprints: Mitarbeiter-Charakteristika
-- Was ARIA über jeden Mitarbeiter gelernt hat
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_employee_fingerprints (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  employee_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Kommunikations-Präferenzen
  information_depth_preference NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = nur die Zahl, 1.0 = vollständige Analyse mit Kontext
  
  decision_speed_preference NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = sehr schnell entscheidend, 1.0 = braucht Zeit und alle Infos
  
  risk_appetite NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = sehr risikoavers, 1.0 = risikofreudig
  
  communication_style VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'balanced',
  -- 'direct', 'diplomatic', 'data_driven', 'narrative', 'balanced'
  
  proactivity_tolerance NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = will nur auf Anfrage Infos, 1.0 = will viele proaktive Hinweise
  
  feedback_culture VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'standard',
  -- 'critical_accepted', 'standard', 'positive_framing_preferred'
  
  tech_affinity NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = tech-skeptisch, 1.0 = tech-enthusiastisch
  
  -- Arbeitszeit-Muster
  typical_start_time TIME,
  typical_end_time TIME,
  lunch_break_pattern VARCHAR(50),
  
  -- Entscheidungs-Stil
  delegation_preference NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = alles selbst entscheiden, 1.0 = delegiert gerne
  
  error_tolerance NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = null Fehlertoleranz, 1.0 = Fehler als Lernchancen
  
  social_orientation NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = sehr aufgabenorientiert, 1.0 = sehr beziehungsorientiert
  
  strategic_vs_operational NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.5,
  -- 0.0 = sehr operational, 1.0 = sehr strategisch
  
  -- Interessen und Expertise
  domain_expertise VARCHAR[],             -- ['amazon_ppc', 'logistics', 'purchasing']
  personal_interests VARCHAR[],           -- Für Rapport: ['football', 'family']
  
  -- ARIA-Interaktions-Statistiken
  total_interactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  positive_reactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  negative_reactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  avg_response_time_seconds INTEGER,      -- Wie schnell reagiert der Mitarbeiter
  most_active_hours INTEGER[],            -- Uhrzeiten (0-23) mit höchster Aktivität
  
  -- Vertrauens-Score
  trust_score NUMERIC(4,3) DEFAULT 0.5,  -- Basiert auf Akzeptanz von ARIA-Empfehlungen
  
  -- Lerngeschwindigkeit (Wie schnell passt sich ARIA an den Mitarbeiter an?)
  model_confidence NUMERIC(4,3) DEFAULT 0.2,  -- 0.0-1.0, steigt mit Interaktionen
  training_interactions_needed INTEGER DEFAULT 50,  -- Bis Fingerprint gut kalibriert
  
  -- Metadaten
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  UNIQUE(tenant_id, employee_id)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_fingerprints_employee ON aria_employee_fingerprints(employee_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_fingerprints_tenant ON aria_employee_fingerprints(tenant_id);

ALTER TABLE aria_employee_fingerprints ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_fingerprints_tenant_isolation ON aria_employee_fingerprints
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_signals: Alle erkannten Signale
-- Der "Sensor-Layer" von ARIA
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_signals (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Signal-Klassifikation
  signal_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  -- 'sales_anomaly', 'inventory_critical', 'supplier_delay', 'competitor_price_change',
  -- 'return_rate_spike', 'revenue_milestone', 'buybox_lost', 'listing_suspended', etc.
  
  severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'medium',
  -- 'info', 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
  
  -- Signal-Inhalt
  title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  
  -- Betroffene Entitäten
  affected_sku VARCHAR(100),
  affected_channel VARCHAR(50),
  affected_employee_id UUID,
  
  -- Metriken
  metric_name VARCHAR(100),              -- Was wurde gemessen
  metric_value NUMERIC,                  -- Aktueller Wert
  metric_expected NUMERIC,              -- Erwarteter Wert
  metric_deviation_percent NUMERIC,      -- % Abweichung
  
  -- Zeitlicher Kontext
  detected_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  started_at TIMESTAMPTZ,               -- Wann hat das Signal begonnen
  ended_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                 -- Falls bereits beendet
  
  -- Status
  status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active',  -- 'active', 'acknowledged', 'resolved', 'false_positive'
  acknowledged_by UUID,
  acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  resolution_note TEXT,
  
  -- ARIA-Bewertung
  confidence NUMERIC(4,3),              -- Wie sicher ist ARIA bei diesem Signal
  is_false_positive BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  false_positive_reason TEXT,
  
  -- Linked Actions
  triggered_actions UUID[],             -- IDs der ausgelösten Actions
  triggered_notifications UUID[],
  
  -- Metadaten
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_tenant ON aria_signals(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_severity ON aria_signals(severity, status);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_type ON aria_signals(signal_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_detected ON aria_signals(detected_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_sku ON aria_signals(affected_sku) WHERE affected_sku IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_signals_active ON aria_signals(tenant_id, status) WHERE status = 'active';

ALTER TABLE aria_signals ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_signals_tenant_isolation ON aria_signals
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_actions: Alle ARIA-Aktionen
-- Was ARIA getan hat oder tun möchte
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_actions (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Aktion-Klassifikation
  action_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  -- 'reorder_proposal', 'bid_adjustment', 'price_change', 'notification_sent',
  -- 'listing_update', 'supplier_contact', 'report_generated', etc.
  
  autonomy_level INTEGER NOT NULL,       -- 0=verboten, 1=einmal-erlaubt, 2=reporting, 3=autonom
  
  -- Aktion-Inhalt
  title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  
  -- Parameter
  parameters JSONB DEFAULT '{}',         -- Aktion-spezifische Parameter
  
  -- Auslöser
  triggered_by_signal_id UUID REFERENCES aria_signals(id),
  triggered_by_employee_id UUID,
  triggered_by_schedule VARCHAR(100),    -- Falls durch Cron
  
  -- Status-Flow
  status VARCHAR(30) DEFAULT 'proposed',
  -- 'proposed', 'pending_approval', 'approved', 'executing', 'completed', 'failed', 'rejected'
  
  -- Genehmigung
  requires_approval BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  approved_by UUID,
  approved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  rejected_by UUID,
  rejected_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  rejection_reason TEXT,
  
  -- Ausführung
  proposed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  executed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  
  -- Ergebnis
  success BOOLEAN,
  result JSONB,                          -- Aktion-Ergebnis
  error_message TEXT,                    -- Falls fehlgeschlagen
  
  -- Auswirkung (für Lernen)
  estimated_impact JSONB,               -- Erwartete Auswirkung
  actual_impact JSONB,                   -- Gemessene tatsächliche Auswirkung (nachträglich)
  impact_measured_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  
  -- Metadaten
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_actions_tenant ON aria_actions(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_actions_status ON aria_actions(status, tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_actions_type ON aria_actions(action_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_actions_proposed ON aria_actions(proposed_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_actions_pending ON aria_actions(tenant_id, status) WHERE status = 'pending_approval';

ALTER TABLE aria_actions ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_actions_tenant_isolation ON aria_actions
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_predictions: Prophylaktisches Gedächtnis
-- Was ARIA vorhergesagt hat und ob es stimmt
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_predictions (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Vorhersage-Art
  prediction_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  -- 'demand_forecast', 'stockout_risk', 'supplier_delay', 'revenue_projection',
  -- 'return_rate', 'price_movement', 'competitor_action', 'seasonal_peak'
  
  -- Kontext
  entity_type VARCHAR(50),               -- 'sku', 'supplier', 'channel', 'tenant'
  entity_id VARCHAR(255),
  entity_name VARCHAR(500),
  
  -- Vorhersage-Inhalt
  prediction_text TEXT NOT NULL,         -- Lesbare Vorhersage
  predicted_value NUMERIC,              -- Quantitative Vorhersage
  predicted_unit VARCHAR(50),           -- Einheit
  confidence NUMERIC(4,3),              -- 0.0-1.0
  
  -- Zeitrahmen
  predicted_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  prediction_horizon_start TIMESTAMPTZ,  -- Ab wann gilt die Vorhersage
  prediction_horizon_end TIMESTAMPTZ,    -- Bis wann gilt die Vorhersage
  
  -- Eintritts-Wahrscheinlichkeit
  probability_low NUMERIC(4,3),          -- Untere Grenze
  probability_mid NUMERIC(4,3),          -- Mittlere Schätzung
  probability_high NUMERIC(4,3),         -- Obere Grenze
  
  -- Empfehlung
  recommended_action TEXT,
  action_deadline TIMESTAMPTZ,           -- Bis wann Handlung empfohlen
  
  -- Evaluierung (ex-post)
  evaluated_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  actual_value NUMERIC,
  prediction_error_percent NUMERIC,      -- % Abweichung von Realität
  was_correct BOOLEAN,                   -- War die Vorhersage-Richtung korrekt
  evaluation_notes TEXT,
  
  -- Metadaten
  model_version VARCHAR(50),             -- Welches Modell wurde verwendet
  training_data_points INTEGER,          -- Wie viele Datenpunkte im Training
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_predictions_tenant ON aria_predictions(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_predictions_type ON aria_predictions(prediction_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_predictions_horizon ON aria_predictions(prediction_horizon_end);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_predictions_entity ON aria_predictions(entity_id, entity_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_predictions_not_evaluated ON aria_predictions(tenant_id) 
  WHERE evaluated_at IS NULL AND prediction_horizon_end < NOW();

ALTER TABLE aria_predictions ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_predictions_tenant_isolation ON aria_predictions
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_sentiment: Emotionaler Gedächtnis-Layer
-- Wie geht es den Mitarbeitern — mit ethischen Schutzmaßnahmen
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_sentiment (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  employee_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Zeitraum (täglich aggregiert, nicht pro Nachricht)
  date DATE NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,
  
  -- Indikatoren (alle 0.0-1.0, normalisiert gegen Baseline)
  work_pace_index NUMERIC(4,3),          -- Arbeitstempo relativ zu Baseline
  response_time_index NUMERIC(4,3),      -- Reaktionszeiten
  error_rate_index NUMERIC(4,3),         -- Fehlerrate
  task_avoidance_index NUMERIC(4,3),     -- Aufgaben-Vermeidungsverhalten
  communication_brevity_index NUMERIC(4,3),  -- Wie kurz sind Nachrichten
  overtime_hours NUMERIC(4,2),           -- Überstunden heute
  decision_uncertainty_index NUMERIC(4,3),  -- Entscheidungs-Zögerlichkeit
  
  -- Zusammenfassung
  overall_stress_score NUMERIC(4,3),     -- Zusammenfassung aller Indikatoren
  anomaly_detected BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  anomaly_description TEXT,
  
  -- ARIA-Reaktion
  aria_response VARCHAR(50),             -- 'none', 'support_offered', 'workload_reduced', 'alert_sent'
  aria_response_details TEXT,
  
  -- Einschränkungen (ethische Schutzmechanismen)
  -- Diese Daten werden NIEMALS für HR-Entscheidungen verwendet
  -- Diese Daten sind NUR für proaktive Unterstützung durch ARIA
  shared_with_hr BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,  -- Immer false — kann nicht auf true gesetzt werden
  shared_with_gf BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,  -- Nur wenn Mitarbeiter explizit zustimmt
  
  -- Datenschutz
  retention_days INTEGER DEFAULT 90,     -- Automatisch gelöscht nach 90 Tagen
  expires_at DATE DEFAULT (CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '90 days'),
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  UNIQUE(tenant_id, employee_id, date)
);

-- Automatisches Löschen nach Retention-Period
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_sentiment_expiry ON aria_sentiment(expires_at);

-- Zusätzlicher Schutz: Nur der Mitarbeiter selbst und ARIA können lesen
ALTER TABLE aria_sentiment ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_sentiment_employee_only ON aria_sentiment
  FOR SELECT USING (
    employee_id = auth.uid() OR  -- Mitarbeiter selbst
    tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID  -- Service-Client für ARIA
  );

-- ############################################################################
-- SEKTION 2: CROSS-TENANT-INTELLIGENZ (Anonymisiert)
-- ############################################################################

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_market_benchmarks: Anonymisierte Cluster-Benchmarks
-- Kein Tenant-FK — vollständig anonymisiert
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_market_benchmarks (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  
  -- Klassifikation (kein Tenant-FK!)
  cluster_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,      -- z.B. 'dach_ecommerce_baby_small'
  cluster_description VARCHAR(500),
  
  -- Zusammensetzung (mindestens 20 Tenants!)
  tenant_count INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (tenant_count >= 20),  -- Anonymitäts-Schutz
  data_period_start DATE,
  data_period_end DATE,
  
  -- Benchmark-Metriken
  metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  
  -- Statistische Verteilung
  p10 NUMERIC,                           -- 10. Perzentil
  p25 NUMERIC,                           -- 25. Perzentil (unteres Quartil)
  p50 NUMERIC,                           -- Median
  p75 NUMERIC,                           -- 75. Perzentil (oberes Quartil)
  p90 NUMERIC,                           -- 90. Perzentil
  mean NUMERIC,                          -- Durchschnitt
  std_dev NUMERIC,                       -- Standardabweichung
  
  -- Einheit und Kontext
  unit VARCHAR(50),
  seasonal_adjustment NUMERIC DEFAULT 1.0,
  
  -- Validität
  computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  valid_until TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT (NOW() + INTERVAL '7 days'),
  
  -- Qualität
  data_quality_score NUMERIC(4,3)        -- Wie verlässlich sind diese Benchmarks
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_benchmarks_cluster ON aria_market_benchmarks(cluster_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_benchmarks_metric ON aria_market_benchmarks(metric_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_benchmarks_validity ON aria_market_benchmarks(valid_until);

-- Benchmarks: KEINE RLS — sie sind bewusst cross-tenant
-- Aber: Nur Service-Client kann schreiben; alle Tenants können lesen

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_emerging_patterns: Neue Muster die ARIA marktübergreifend erkennt
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_emerging_patterns (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  
  -- Muster-Beschreibung
  pattern_name VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL,
  pattern_type VARCHAR(100),             -- 'demand_shift', 'regulatory', 'competitor', 'seasonal'
  
  description TEXT NOT NULL,
  affected_categories VARCHAR[],         -- Betroffene Produktkategorien
  affected_channels VARCHAR[],           -- Betroffene Marktplätze
  affected_regions VARCHAR[],            -- Betroffene Regionen
  
  -- Evidenz
  supporting_tenant_count INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (supporting_tenant_count >= 5),
  first_detected_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  confidence NUMERIC(4,3),
  
  -- Zeitrahmen
  trend_direction VARCHAR(20),           -- 'rising', 'falling', 'stable', 'volatile'
  estimated_peak_date DATE,
  duration_weeks_estimate INTEGER,
  
  -- Handlungs-Empfehlung
  recommended_action TEXT,
  action_urgency VARCHAR(20),            -- 'immediate', 'this_week', 'this_month', 'monitor'
  
  -- Benachrichtigungs-Status
  tenant_notifications_sent INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ############################################################################
-- SEKTION 3: KOMMUNIKATION & BENACHRICHTIGUNGEN
-- ############################################################################

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_notifications: Alle ARIA-Benachrichtigungen
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_notifications (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Empfänger
  recipient_employee_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  recipient_role VARCHAR(50),            -- Falls an alle in einer Rolle
  
  -- Inhalt
  notification_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
  message TEXT NOT NULL,
  
  -- Priorität und Kanal
  priority VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'medium',  -- 'critical', 'high', 'medium', 'low', 'info'
  channel VARCHAR(30) DEFAULT 'in_app',  -- 'in_app', 'push', 'email', 'sms'
  
  -- Referenzen
  related_signal_id UUID REFERENCES aria_signals(id),
  related_action_id UUID REFERENCES aria_actions(id),
  related_episode_id UUID REFERENCES aria_episodes(id),
  
  -- Delivery
  sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  delivered_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  read_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  
  -- Reaktion
  user_reaction VARCHAR(30),             -- 'accepted', 'rejected', 'ignored', 'deferred'
  user_reaction_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  user_reaction_note TEXT,
  
  -- Anti-Spam
  bundle_id UUID,                        -- Falls Teil eines Bundles
  is_bundled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  
  -- Lern-Signal
  was_relevant BOOLEAN,                  -- War diese Notification relevant? (Feedback)
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_notifications_tenant ON aria_notifications(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_notifications_employee ON aria_notifications(recipient_employee_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_notifications_unread ON aria_notifications(tenant_id, read_at) WHERE read_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_notifications_priority ON aria_notifications(priority, sent_at DESC);

ALTER TABLE aria_notifications ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_notifications_tenant_isolation ON aria_notifications
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_notification_rate_limits: Anti-Spam System
-- Verhindert dass ARIA den Mitarbeiter bombardiert
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_notification_rate_limits (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  employee_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Zeitfenster
  window_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,      -- 'hourly', 'daily', 'weekly'
  window_start TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  
  -- Limits
  notifications_sent INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  max_allowed INTEGER DEFAULT 10,        -- Pro Zeitfenster
  critical_override BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,  -- Kritische Alerts ignorieren Limit
  
  -- Pro Notification-Typ
  counts_by_type JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  
  -- Nutzer-Präferenzen
  quiet_hours_start TIME DEFAULT '20:00',
  quiet_hours_end TIME DEFAULT '07:00',
  quiet_hours_timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'Europe/Berlin',
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  UNIQUE(tenant_id, employee_id, window_type, window_start)
);

-- ############################################################################
-- SEKTION 4: NACHT-MOTOR & BRIEFINGS
-- ############################################################################

-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- aria_morning_briefings: Generierte Morning Briefings
-- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aria_morning_briefings (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  
  -- Empfänger
  recipient_role VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,   -- 'gf', 'vertrieb', 'lager', 'buchhaltung', etc.
  recipient_employee_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  
  -- Zeitraum
  briefing_date DATE NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,
  generated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  -- Inhalt
  headline VARCHAR(500),                 -- Ein-Satz-Zusammenfassung
  content JSONB NOT NULL,               -- Strukturierter Briefing-Inhalt
  content_markdown TEXT,                -- Lesbare Markdown-Version
  
  -- Metriken-Snapshot
  key_metrics JSONB,                     -- Die wichtigsten KPIs des Tages
  
  -- Prioritäten
  top_priority_1 TEXT,
  top_priority_2 TEXT,
  top_priority_3 TEXT,
  
  -- Offene Punkte (Carry-over vom Vortag)
  open_items JSONB,
  
  -- Qualität
  generation_time_ms INTEGER,           -- Wie lange hat die Generierung gedauert
  data_freshness NUMERIC(4,3),          -- 0-1, wie aktuell sind die Daten
  
  -- Delivery
  delivered_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  opened_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  
  -- Feedback
  user_rating INTEGER CHECK (user_rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  user_feedback TEXT,
  
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  UNIQUE(tenant_id, recipient_employee_id, briefing_date)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_aria_briefings_tenant ON aria_morning_briefings(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_briefings_date ON aria_morning_briefings(briefing_date DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_aria_briefings_employee ON aria_morning_briefings(recipient_employee_id, briefing_date DESC);

ALTER TABLE aria_morning_briefings ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY aria_briefings_tenant_isolation ON aria_morning_briefings
  FOR ALL USING (tenant_id = current_setting('app.current_tenant_id')::UUID);

-- ############################################################################
-- SEKTION 5: HILFS-FUNKTIONEN & VIEWS
-- ############################################################################

-- View: ARIA Performance Dashboard
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW aria_performance_dashboard AS
SELECT
  t.id AS tenant_id,
  t.name AS tenant_name,
  
  -- Prediction Accuracy
  (
    SELECT AVG(CASE WHEN was_correct THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END)
    FROM aria_predictions
    WHERE tenant_id = t.id 
    AND evaluated_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
  ) AS prediction_accuracy_30d,
  
  -- Notification Engagement
  (
    SELECT AVG(CASE WHEN user_reaction = 'accepted' THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END)
    FROM aria_notifications
    WHERE tenant_id = t.id
    AND sent_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
    AND user_reaction IS NOT NULL
  ) AS notification_acceptance_rate_30d,
  
  -- Active Signals
  (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM aria_signals
    WHERE tenant_id = t.id
    AND status = 'active'
    AND severity IN ('high', 'critical')
  ) AS active_critical_signals,
  
  -- Knowledge Base Size
  (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM aria_knowledge
    WHERE tenant_id = t.id
    AND valid_until IS NULL OR valid_until > NOW()
  ) AS active_knowledge_count,
  
  -- Episode Count
  (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM aria_episodes
    WHERE tenant_id = t.id
    AND occurred_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
  ) AS episodes_last_30d

FROM tenants t;

-- Funktion: ARIA Kontext für Chat-Anfragen aufbauen
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_aria_context(
  p_tenant_id UUID,
  p_employee_id UUID,
  p_query_text TEXT
)
RETURNS JSONB AS $$
DECLARE
  v_context JSONB;
  v_fingerprint RECORD;
  v_active_signals JSONB;
  v_recent_episodes JSONB;
  v_relevant_knowledge JSONB;
BEGIN
  -- Employee Fingerprint laden
  SELECT * INTO v_fingerprint
  FROM aria_employee_fingerprints
  WHERE tenant_id = p_tenant_id AND employee_id = p_employee_id;
  
  -- Aktive kritische Signale
  SELECT jsonb_agg(jsonb_build_object(
    'type', signal_type,
    'title', title,
    'severity', severity,
    'detected_at', detected_at
  ))
  INTO v_active_signals
  FROM aria_signals
  WHERE tenant_id = p_tenant_id
  AND status = 'active'
  AND severity IN ('high', 'critical')
  ORDER BY detected_at DESC
  LIMIT 5;
  
  -- Relevante Episoden (Volltextsuche)
  SELECT jsonb_agg(jsonb_build_object(
    'title', title,
    'outcome', outcome,
    'occurred_at', occurred_at,
    'lessons', lessons_learned
  ))
  INTO v_recent_episodes
  FROM aria_episodes
  WHERE tenant_id = p_tenant_id
  AND search_vector @@ plainto_tsquery('german', p_query_text)
  ORDER BY importance_score DESC, occurred_at DESC
  LIMIT 5;
  
  -- Relevantes Wissen
  SELECT jsonb_agg(jsonb_build_object(
    'fact', fact,
    'confidence', confidence,
    'type', knowledge_type
  ))
  INTO v_relevant_knowledge
  FROM aria_knowledge
  WHERE tenant_id = p_tenant_id
  AND (valid_until IS NULL OR valid_until > NOW())
  AND search_vector @@ plainto_tsquery('german', p_query_text)
  ORDER BY confidence DESC, last_confirmed_at DESC
  LIMIT 10;
  
  -- Kontext zusammenbauen
  v_context := jsonb_build_object(
    'employee', jsonb_build_object(
      'id', p_employee_id,
      'info_depth_preference', COALESCE(v_fingerprint.information_depth_preference, 0.5),
      'communication_style', COALESCE(v_fingerprint.communication_style, 'balanced'),
      'proactivity_tolerance', COALESCE(v_fingerprint.proactivity_tolerance, 0.5),
      'trust_score', COALESCE(v_fingerprint.trust_score, 0.5)
    ),
    'active_signals', COALESCE(v_active_signals, '[]'::jsonb),
    'relevant_episodes', COALESCE(v_recent_episodes, '[]'::jsonb),
    'relevant_knowledge', COALESCE(v_relevant_knowledge, '[]'::jsonb)
  );
  
  RETURN v_context;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

-- Trigger: Automatisches Löschen von Sentiment-Daten nach Retention
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION cleanup_expired_sentiment()
RETURNS void AS $$
BEGIN
  DELETE FROM aria_sentiment
  WHERE expires_at < CURRENT_DATE;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Grant Statements
GRANT SELECT ON aria_market_benchmarks TO authenticated;
GRANT SELECT ON aria_emerging_patterns TO authenticated;
GRANT ALL ON aria_episodes TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_knowledge TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_signals TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_actions TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_notifications TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_predictions TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_employee_fingerprints TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_morning_briefings TO service_role;
GRANT ALL ON aria_sentiment TO service_role;
GRANT SELECT ON aria_performance_dashboard TO service_role;
GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION get_aria_context TO service_role;
```

# TEIL AA — VOLLSTÄNDIGE BULLMQ WORKER-IMPLEMENTIERUNGEN

> Jeder BullMQ-Job vollständig implementiert — Production-ready.

---

## AA.1 Job-Registry — Alle 20 ARIA-Jobs

```typescript
// /src/lib/aria/jobs/registry.ts

import { Queue, Worker, QueueScheduler } from 'bullmq';
import { getRedis } from '@/lib/redis';

// ============================================================
// QUEUE-DEFINITIONEN
// ============================================================

export const ARIA_QUEUES = {
  // Echtzeit-Verarbeitung (höchste Priorität)
  SIGNAL_PROCESSOR: 'aria:signal-processor',
  NOTIFICATION_ROUTER: 'aria:notification-router',
  ACTION_EXECUTOR: 'aria:action-executor',
  
  // Stündliche Jobs
  INVENTORY_MONITOR: 'aria:inventory-monitor',
  ORDER_SYNC: 'aria:order-sync',
  PRICE_MONITOR: 'aria:price-monitor',
  
  // Mehrmals täglich
  COMPETITOR_WATCH: 'aria:competitor-watch',
  PPC_OPTIMIZER: 'aria:ppc-optimizer',
  DEMAND_FORECASTER: 'aria:demand-forecaster',
  
  // Täglich
  MORNING_BRIEFING: 'aria:morning-briefing',
  KNOWLEDGE_EXTRACTOR: 'aria:knowledge-extractor',
  ANOMALY_DETECTOR: 'aria:anomaly-detector',
  BENCHMARK_UPDATER: 'aria:benchmark-updater',
  FINGERPRINT_TRAINER: 'aria:fingerprint-trainer',
  
  // Wöchentlich
  STRATEGIC_REPORT: 'aria:strategic-report',
  SUPPLIER_REVIEW: 'aria:supplier-review',
  KNOWLEDGE_DECAY: 'aria:knowledge-decay',
  PREDICTION_EVALUATOR: 'aria:prediction-evaluator',
  
  // Nacht-Motor
  NIGHT_PROCESSOR: 'aria:night-processor',
  SENTIMENT_ANALYZER: 'aria:sentiment-analyzer',
} as const;

export function createAriaQueues() {
  const redis = getRedis();
  
  return Object.entries(ARIA_QUEUES).reduce((acc, [name, queueName]) => ({
    ...acc,
    [name]: new Queue(queueName, { connection: redis })
  }), {} as Record<keyof typeof ARIA_QUEUES, Queue>);
}
```

## AA.2 Signal-Processor Worker — Vollständig

```typescript
// /src/lib/aria/workers/signal-processor.worker.ts

import { Worker, Job } from 'bullmq';
import { createServiceClient } from '@/lib/supabase';
import { getRedis } from '@/lib/redis';

interface SignalProcessorJob {
  tenantId: string;
  signalType: string;
  data: Record<string, unknown>;
  triggeredBy: 'cron' | 'webhook' | 'manual';
}

export function createSignalProcessorWorker() {
  const redis = getRedis();
  
  return new Worker<SignalProcessorJob>(
    'aria:signal-processor',
    async (job: Job<SignalProcessorJob>) => {
      const { tenantId, signalType, data } = job.data;
      const supabase = createServiceClient();
      
      console.log(`[ARIA Signal] Processing ${signalType} for tenant ${tenantId}`);
      
      try {
        // 1. Signal analysieren
        const analysis = await analyzeSignal(signalType, data, tenantId);
        
        // 2. Ist das ein echtes Signal oder Rauschen?
        if (!analysis.isSignificant) {
          await job.updateProgress({ status: 'dismissed', reason: analysis.dismissReason });
          return;
        }
        
        // 3. Signal in DB speichern
        const { data: signal, error } = await supabase
          .from('aria_signals')
          .insert({
            tenant_id: tenantId,
            signal_type: signalType,
            severity: analysis.severity,
            title: analysis.title,
            description: analysis.description,
            metric_name: analysis.metricName,
            metric_value: analysis.metricValue,
            metric_expected: analysis.metricExpected,
            metric_deviation_percent: analysis.deviationPercent,
            confidence: analysis.confidence
          })
          .select()
          .single();
        
        if (error) throw error;
        
        // 4. Episodisches Gedächtnis updaten
        await recordEpisode(tenantId, {
          type: signalType,
          title: analysis.title,
          importance: analysis.severity === 'critical' ? 0.9 : 
                      analysis.severity === 'high' ? 0.7 :
                      analysis.severity === 'medium' ? 0.5 : 0.3
        });
        
        // 5. Notification-Routing triggern
        if (analysis.severity !== 'info') {
          await job.queue.add('notify', {
            tenantId,
            signalId: signal.id,
            severity: analysis.severity,
            targetRoles: analysis.relevantRoles,
          }, { priority: analysis.severity === 'critical' ? 1 : 5 });
        }
        
        // 6. Action-Vorschlag generieren
        if (analysis.suggestedAction) {
          await generateActionProposal(tenantId, signal.id, analysis.suggestedAction);
        }
        
        await job.updateProgress({ status: 'completed', signalId: signal.id });
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`[ARIA Signal] Error processing ${signalType}:`, error);
        throw error;  // BullMQ handled retry
      }
    },
    {
      connection: redis,
      concurrency: 10,  // 10 parallele Signal-Verarbeitungen
      limiter: {
        max: 100,
        duration: 1000  // Max 100 Jobs pro Sekunde
      }
    }
  );
}

async function analyzeSignal(
  signalType: string, 
  data: Record<string, unknown>,
  tenantId: string
): Promise<SignalAnalysis> {
  
  switch (signalType) {
    case 'inventory_below_threshold':
      return analyzeInventorySignal(data, tenantId);
    
    case 'sales_velocity_anomaly':
      return analyzeSalesVelocitySignal(data, tenantId);
    
    case 'return_rate_spike':
      return analyzeReturnRateSignal(data, tenantId);
    
    case 'buybox_lost':
      return analyzeBuyBoxSignal(data, tenantId);
    
    case 'listing_suspended':
      return analyzeListingSuspensionSignal(data, tenantId);
    
    case 'competitor_price_drop':
      return analyzeCompetitorPriceSignal(data, tenantId);
    
    default:
      return analyzeGenericSignal(signalType, data, tenantId);
  }
}

async function analyzeInventorySignal(
  data: Record<string, unknown>,
  tenantId: string
): Promise<SignalAnalysis> {
  const { sku, currentStock, dailyVelocity } = data as {
    sku: string;
    currentStock: number;
    dailyVelocity: number;
  };
  
  const daysUntilStockout = dailyVelocity > 0 ? currentStock / dailyVelocity : Infinity;
  
  // Severity bestimmen
  let severity: 'critical' | 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' | 'info';
  if (daysUntilStockout <= 1) severity = 'critical';
  else if (daysUntilStockout <= 3) severity = 'high';
  else if (daysUntilStockout <= 7) severity = 'medium';
  else severity = 'low';
  
  // Lieferzeit laden
  const supabase = createServiceClient();
  const { data: supplier } = await supabase
    .from('products')
    .select('supplier_id, lead_time_days')
    .eq('sku', sku)
    .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
    .single();
  
  const leadTime = supplier?.lead_time_days || 7;
  const needsImmediateOrder = daysUntilStockout <= leadTime;
  
  return {
    isSignificant: daysUntilStockout <= 10,
    severity,
    title: `${sku}: Bestand in ${Math.floor(daysUntilStockout)} Tagen erschöpft`,
    description: `Aktueller Bestand: ${currentStock} Einheiten. Verkauf: ${dailyVelocity.toFixed(1)}/Tag. Lieferzeit: ${leadTime} Tage.`,
    metricName: 'days_until_stockout',
    metricValue: daysUntilStockout,
    metricExpected: 14,  // Soll-Puffer
    deviationPercent: ((14 - daysUntilStockout) / 14 * 100),
    confidence: 0.92,
    relevantRoles: ['einkauf', 'gf'],
    suggestedAction: needsImmediateOrder ? {
      type: 'reorder_proposal',
      sku,
      urgency: severity === 'critical' ? 'immediate' : 'today',
      proposedQuantity: Math.ceil(dailyVelocity * 30)  // 30-Tage-Puffer
    } : null
  };
}
```

## AA.3 Morning Briefing Worker — Vollständig

```typescript
// /src/lib/aria/workers/morning-briefing.worker.ts

import { Worker, Job } from 'bullmq';
import Anthropic from '@anthropic-ai/sdk';
import { createServiceClient } from '@/lib/supabase';

interface MorningBriefingJob {
  tenantId: string;
  targetDate: string;  // ISO date string
}

export function createMorningBriefingWorker() {
  const redis = getRedis();
  const anthropic = new Anthropic();
  
  return new Worker<MorningBriefingJob>(
    'aria:morning-briefing',
    async (job: Job<MorningBriefingJob>) => {
      const { tenantId, targetDate } = job.data;
      const supabase = createServiceClient();
      
      // Alle Mitarbeiter des Tenants laden
      const { data: employees } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .select('id, role, name, email')
        .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
        .eq('active', true);
      
      if (!employees?.length) return;
      
      // Für jede Rolle ein individuelles Briefing
      const roleGroups = groupByRole(employees);
      
      for (const [role, roleEmployees] of Object.entries(roleGroups)) {
        await job.updateProgress({ currentRole: role });
        
        // Relevante Daten für diese Rolle laden
        const briefingData = await collectBriefingData(tenantId, role, targetDate);
        
        // ARIA-spezifischen Prompt bauen
        const systemPrompt = buildBriefingSystemPrompt(role);
        const userPrompt = buildBriefingUserPrompt(briefingData, role);
        
        // LLM-Generierung
        const response = await anthropic.messages.create({
          model: 'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001',  // Haiku für Briefings (schnell, günstig)
          max_tokens: 2000,
          system: systemPrompt,
          messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }]
        });
        
        const briefingContent = response.content[0].type === 'text' 
          ? response.content[0].text 
          : '';
        
        // Für jeden Mitarbeiter dieser Rolle speichern
        for (const employee of roleEmployees) {
          // Personalisierung: Fingerprint laden und Briefing anpassen
          const fingerprint = await getEmployeeFingerprint(employee.id);
          const personalizedContent = personalizeBriefing(briefingContent, fingerprint);
          
          await supabase.from('aria_morning_briefings').upsert({
            tenant_id: tenantId,
            recipient_role: role,
            recipient_employee_id: employee.id,
            briefing_date: targetDate,
            content_markdown: personalizedContent,
            key_metrics: briefingData.keyMetrics,
            top_priority_1: briefingData.priorities[0],
            top_priority_2: briefingData.priorities[1],
            top_priority_3: briefingData.priorities[2],
            generation_time_ms: Date.now() - job.timestamp
          }, { onConflict: 'tenant_id,recipient_employee_id,briefing_date' });
        }
      }
    },
    { connection: redis, concurrency: 3 }
  );
}

async function collectBriefingData(
  tenantId: string, 
  role: string, 
  date: string
): Promise<BriefingData> {
  const supabase = createServiceClient();
  const targetDate = new Date(date);
  const yesterday = subDays(targetDate, 1);
  const lastWeek = subDays(targetDate, 7);
  
  // Basis-Metriken (für alle Rollen)
  const { data: ordersYesterday } = await supabase
    .from('orders')
    .select('id, total_gross, status, channel')
    .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
    .gte('ordered_at', yesterday.toISOString())
    .lt('ordered_at', targetDate.toISOString());
  
  // Aktive kritische Signale
  const { data: criticalSignals } = await supabase
    .from('aria_signals')
    .select('*')
    .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
    .eq('status', 'active')
    .in('severity', ['critical', 'high'])
    .order('detected_at', { ascending: false })
    .limit(5);
  
  // Offene Aktionen (pending_approval)
  const { data: pendingActions } = await supabase
    .from('aria_actions')
    .select('*')
    .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
    .eq('status', 'pending_approval')
    .order('proposed_at', { ascending: false });
  
  // Rolle-spezifische Daten
  let roleSpecificData = {};
  
  switch (role) {
    case 'gf':
      roleSpecificData = await collectGFData(supabase, tenantId, yesterday, lastWeek);
      break;
    case 'einkauf':
      roleSpecificData = await collectEinkaufData(supabase, tenantId);
      break;
    case 'lager':
      roleSpecificData = await collectLagerData(supabase, tenantId, targetDate);
      break;
    case 'buchhaltung':
      roleSpecificData = await collectBuchhaltungData(supabase, tenantId, yesterday);
      break;
    case 'vertrieb':
      roleSpecificData = await collectVertriebData(supabase, tenantId, yesterday);
      break;
  }
  
  return {
    date,
    role,
    orders: ordersYesterday || [],
    criticalSignals: criticalSignals || [],
    pendingActions: pendingActions || [],
    keyMetrics: calculateKeyMetrics(ordersYesterday || []),
    priorities: extractPriorities(criticalSignals || [], pendingActions || [], role),
    ...roleSpecificData
  };
}

function buildBriefingSystemPrompt(role: string): string {
  const roleInstructions = {
    gf: `Du bist ARIA, der KI-Kollege des Geschäftsführers. 
Dein Morning Briefing für den GF ist:
- Maximal 1 A4-Seite (Markdown)
- Struktur: Gestern (Zahlen) → Heute (Prioritäten) → ARIA empfiehlt
- Ton: Direkt, zahlenbasiert, keine Floskeln
- Erster Satz: immer die wichtigste Zahl des gestrigen Tages
- Keine Passivkonstruktionen. Keine "Es könnte sein". Klare Aussagen.`,
    
    einkauf: `Du bist ARIA für den Einkäufer.
- Fokus: Was muss heute bestellt werden? Was läuft aus?
- Priorität 1: Kritische Bestände (Stockout < 48h)
- Priorität 2: Bestellvorschläge mit konkreten Mengen
- Kein strategisches Gerede — nur operative Handlungen`,
    
    lager: `Du bist ARIA für den Lageristen.
- Fokus: Was kommt heute rein? Was muss raus?
- Lieferungen heute (genaue Uhrzeiten wenn bekannt)
- Offene Kommissionieraufgaben
- Retouren von gestern (Status)
- Kurz, klar, in Stichpunkten`,
    
    buchhaltung: `Du bist ARIA für die Buchhaltung.
- Fokus: Offene Posten, fällige Zahlungen, Anomalien
- Eingangsrechnungen die heute geprüft werden müssen
- Zahlungen die heute ausgehen sollen
- Liquiditätsstatus
- Zahlengenau, keine Unschärfen`,
    
    vertrieb: `Du bist ARIA für das Vertriebsteam.
- Fokus: Welche Kunden brauchen heute Aufmerksamkeit?
- Geplante Besuche (kurze Briefings)
- Offene Angebote mit Deadline
- Neue Leads oder Opportunities
- Beziehungsorientiert, aber faktenbasiert`
  };
  
  return `Du bist ARIA — der intelligente KI-Kollege von Comentra.

${roleInstructions[role] || roleInstructions.gf}

ARIA-Sprachregeln:
- Zahlen immer vor Wörtern
- Keine Passivkonstruktionen  
- Empfehlungen immer konkret und ausführbar
- Unsicherheit quantifizieren ("68% Wahrscheinlichkeit") statt verstecken ("könnte sein")
- Kein "Guten Morgen", kein "Ich hoffe du hattest einen guten Start" — direkt in die Inhalte
`;
}
```

## AA.4 Demand Forecasting Worker

```typescript
// /src/lib/aria/workers/demand-forecaster.worker.ts

export function createDemandForecasterWorker() {
  const redis = getRedis();
  
  return new Worker(
    'aria:demand-forecaster',
    async (job: Job) => {
      const { tenantId } = job.data;
      const supabase = createServiceClient();
      
      // Alle aktiven SKUs des Tenants
      const { data: products } = await supabase
        .from('products')
        .select('sku, name, category, lead_time_days')
        .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
        .eq('active', true);
      
      if (!products?.length) return;
      
      let processedCount = 0;
      
      for (const product of products) {
        // Verkaufshistorie laden
        const { data: salesHistory } = await supabase
          .from('order_items')
          .select('quantity, ordered_at')
          .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
          .eq('sku', product.sku)
          .gte('ordered_at', subDays(new Date(), 365).toISOString())
          .order('ordered_at', { ascending: true });
        
        if (!salesHistory?.length || salesHistory.length < 14) {
          // Zu wenig Daten
          processedCount++;
          continue;
        }
        
        // Daily aggregation
        const dailySales = aggregateToDailyBuckets(salesHistory);
        
        // Trend berechnen
        const trend = calculateLinearTrend(dailySales.map(d => d.quantity));
        
        // Saisonalität extrahieren
        const seasonality = extractSeasonality(dailySales);
        
        // 30-Tage-Forecast
        const forecast = generateForecast(dailySales, trend, seasonality, 30);
        
        // Reorder Point berechnen
        const leadTime = product.lead_time_days || 7;
        const safetyStock = calculateSafetyStock(dailySales, leadTime);
        const reorderPoint = Math.ceil(
          forecast.slice(0, leadTime).reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.demand, 0) + safetyStock
        );
        
        // EOQ berechnen (Economic Order Quantity)
        const annualDemand = forecast.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.demand, 0) * 12;
        const eoq = calculateEOQ(annualDemand, product.sku);
        
        // Prediction speichern
        await supabase.from('aria_predictions').insert({
          tenant_id: tenantId,
          prediction_type: 'demand_forecast',
          entity_type: 'sku',
          entity_id: product.sku,
          entity_name: product.name,
          prediction_text: `30-Tage-Forecast: ${forecast.reduce((s,f) => s + f.demand, 0).toFixed(0)} Einheiten. Nachbestellung wenn Bestand unter ${reorderPoint}.`,
          predicted_value: reorderPoint,
          predicted_unit: 'Einheiten (Reorder Point)',
          confidence: Math.min(0.95, 0.4 + (salesHistory.length / 365) * 0.55),
          prediction_horizon_start: new Date(),
          prediction_horizon_end: addDays(new Date(), 30),
          recommended_action: `Nachbestellung: ${eoq} Einheiten wenn Bestand = ${reorderPoint}`
        });
        
        processedCount++;
        await job.updateProgress({ processed: processedCount, total: products.length });
      }
      
      console.log(`[ARIA Forecast] Completed ${processedCount} SKU forecasts for tenant ${tenantId}`);
    },
    { connection: redis, concurrency: 2 }
  );
}
```

## AA.5 Competitor Watcher Worker

```typescript
// /src/lib/aria/workers/competitor-watcher.worker.ts

export function createCompetitorWatcherWorker() {
  const redis = getRedis();
  
  return new Worker(
    'aria:competitor-watch',
    async (job: Job) => {
      const { tenantId } = job.data;
      const supabase = createServiceClient();
      
      // Unsere Listings mit Wettbewerber-Tracking
      const { data: listings } = await supabase
        .from('channel_listings')
        .select('sku, channel, external_id, current_price')
        .eq('tenant_id', tenantId)
        .eq('competitor_tracking_enabled', true);
      
      if (!listings?.length) return;
      
      for (const listing of listings) {
        try {
          let competitors: CompetitorListing[] = [];
          
          if (listing.channel === 'amazon') {
            competitors = await getAmazonCompetitors(listing.external_id);
          } else if (listing.channel === 'ebay') {
            competitors = await getEbayCompetitors(listing.external_id);
          }
          
          if (!competitors.length) continue;
          
          // Preis-Position analysieren
          const prices = competitors.map(c => c.price).sort((a, b) => a - b);
          const ourRank = prices.filter(p => p < listing.current_price).length + 1;
          const ourPercentile = ourRank / prices.length;
          
          // Signifikante Änderung?
          const cheapestCompetitor = prices[0];
          const previousCheapest = await getPreviousCheapestCompetitor(tenantId, listing.sku, listing.channel);
          
          if (previousCheapest && Math.abs(cheapestCompetitor - previousCheapest) / previousCheapest > 0.05) {
            // >5% Preisänderung beim günstigsten Konkurrenten — Signal erzeugen
            await signalQueue.add('signal', {
              tenantId,
              signalType: 'competitor_price_change',
              data: {
                sku: listing.sku,
                channel: listing.channel,
                ourPrice: listing.current_price,
                newCheapestPrice: cheapestCompetitor,
                oldCheapestPrice: previousCheapest,
                changePercent: ((cheapestCompetitor - previousCheapest) / previousCheapest * 100)
              }
            });
          }
          
          // Wettbewerber-Snapshot in Redis cachen
          await redis.setex(
            `competitor:${tenantId}:${listing.channel}:${listing.sku}`,
            3600 * 6,  // 6 Stunden
            JSON.stringify({ prices, cheapest: cheapestCompetitor, updatedAt: new Date() })
          );
          
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`[ARIA Competitor] Failed for ${listing.sku} on ${listing.channel}:`, error);
        }
      }
    },
    { connection: redis, concurrency: 5 }
  );
}
```
